  <raw>Europe stocks edge up as Fed decision looms




MADRID (MarketWatch) -- European stocks moved cautiously higher Wednesday, as markets awaited the outcome of the U.S. Federal Reserve's monetary-meeting and mulled China factory data that showed some weak spots. Purchasing-manager surveys will also be relaesed Wednesday in Europe. The Stoxx Europe 600 index (xx:sxxp) rose 0.3% to 262.05, led by a 1.2% rise for HSBC Holdings PLC (uk:hsba)  (hbc) . Standard Chartered PLC (uk:stan) rose 2.33% on the back of earnings. The FTSE 100 index (uk:ukx) rose 0.4% to 5,658.49. French banks were also boosting the CAC 40 index (fr:px1) , up 0.6% to 3,311.92. Shares of Societe Generale SA (fr:aca) rose 2.7% after the French bank posted a profit fall but was upbeat. The German DAX 30 index (dx:dax) rose 0.1% to 6,780.58, with BMW AG (de:bmw) down 2.7% after posting a profit fall.
